if (!theForm) {
    theForm = document.FormPortal;

function __doPostBack(eventTarget, eventArgument) {
    if (!theForm.onsubmit || (theForm.onsubmit() != false)) {
        theForm.__EVENTTARGET.value = eventTarget;
        theForm.__EVENTARGUMENT.value = eventArgument;
        theForm.submit();
    }
}

<script language='javascript'>function GetElement(myElement){  if (document.getElementById)    return document.getElementById(myElement)  else    return document.all[myElement]} </script><script language='javascript'>function GetXmlHttpObject(){  var xmlHttp=null;  try  {    // Firefox, Opera 8.0+, Safari    xmlHttp=new XMLHttpRequest();  }  catch (e)  {    // Internet Explorer    try    {      xmlHttp=new ActiveXObject('Msxml2.XMLHTTP');    }    catch (e)    {      xmlHttp=new ActiveXObject('Microsoft.XMLHTTP');    }  } return xmlHttp;} </script><script type='text/javascript'>
var historyHash = 0;
var historyPos = [0,0];
function addHistory(myHash)
{
  historyHash = myHash;
  historyPos = getScrollingPosition();
  Sys.Application.addHistoryPoint({value: myHash}, 'e-stave.com');
}
function onStateChanged(sender, e)
{
  var val = parseInt(e.get_state().value || '0'); 
  if ((historyHash != 0) && (val != historyHash))
  {
    historyHash = val;
    if (typeof(doBack) == 'function') doBack();
      {
          doBack();
          window.scrollTo(0, historyPos[1]);
      }
  }
}
function getScrollingPosition() {
	var position = [0, 0];
	if (typeof window.pageYOffset != 'undefined') {
		position = [
			window.pageXOffset,
			window.pageYOffset
		];
	} else if (typeof document.documentElement.scrollTop
		 != 'undefined' && document.documentElement.scrollTop > 0) {
		position = [
			document.documentElement.scrollLeft,
			document.documentElement.scrollTop
		];
	} else if (typeof document.body.scrollTop != 'undefined') {
		position = [
			document.body.scrollLeft,
			document.body.scrollTop
		];
	}
	return position;
}
</script>

function iShowPopUp(strDialog, strCover)
{
  if (strCover == undefined)
    cvr = GetElement('coverDivPopuUp');
  else
    cvr = GetElement(strCover);
  dlg = GetElement(strDialog);
  divh = dlg.offsetHeight;
  divhalf = '-'+ divh/2;
  dlg.style.marginTop= divhalf + 'px';
  cvr.style.display = 'block';
  dlg.style.display = 'block';
  cvr.style.width = '100%'
  cvr.style.height = '100%'
}
function iClosePopUp(strDialog, strCover)
{
  if (strCover == undefined)
    cvr = GetElement('coverDivPopuUp');
  else
    cvr = GetElement(strCover);
  dlg = GetElement(strDialog);
  cvr.style.display = 'none';
  dlg.style.display = 'none';
}
</script>
<script language='javascript'>
function numbersOnly(e)
{
  var evt = (e) ? e : window.event;
  var key = (evt.keyCode) ? evt.keyCode : evt.which;
  if(key != null)
  {
    key = parseInt(key, 10);
    if((key < 48 || key > 57) && (key < 96 || key > 105))
    {
      if(!isUserFriendlyChar(key))
        return false;
    }
    else
    {
      if(evt.shiftKey)
        return false;
    }
  }
  return true;
}
function isUserFriendlyChar(val)
{
  if(val == 8 || val == 9 || val == 13 || val == 45 || val == 46 || val == 110 || val == 188)
    return true;
  if((val > 16 && val < 21) || (val > 34 && val < 41))
    return true;
  return false;
}
 </script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function toggleSelekcija(SelekcijaContent, SelekcijaExpand, cssExpand, cssContract)
{
  if (GetElement(SelekcijaContent) == null)
    return;
  var strClassName = GetElement(SelekcijaContent).className;
  if (strClassName.indexOf(' hidden') > -1)
  {
    strClassName = strClassName.replace(' hidden', '');
    GetElement(SelekcijaContent).className = strClassName;
    GetElement(SelekcijaExpand).className = cssContract;
  }
  else
  {
    strClassName += ' hidden';
    GetElement(SelekcijaContent).className = strClassName;
    GetElement(SelekcijaExpand).className = cssExpand;
  }
  event.cancelBubble = true;
}
function closeSelekcija(SelekcijaContent)
{
  if (GetElement(SelekcijaContent) != null)
  {
    var strClassName = GetElement(SelekcijaContent).className;
    if (strClassName.indexOf(' hidden') == -1)
      strClassName += ' hidden';
    GetElement(SelekcijaContent).className = strClassName;
  }
}
</script>

<script language='javascript'>
function windowOpen(AWindow, name, url, width, height, params, left, top)
{
  var newwindow =  null;
  if (AWindow != null) 
  {
    newwindow = AWindow;
    newwindow.location.href = url;
  }
  else 
  {
    var strParams =  'width=' + width + ',height=' + height;
    leftVal = (left !='undefined' ? left : (screen.width - width) / 2);
    if (leftVal < 0)
      leftVal = 0;
    topVal = (top !='undefined' ? top : (screen.height - height) / 2);
    if (topVal < 0) 
      topVal = 0;
    strParams = strParams + ',left=' + leftVal + ',top=' + topVal;
    if (params != '') 
      strParams = strParams + ',' + params;
    newwindow = window.open(url, name, strParams);
  }
  newwindow.focus();
}
 </script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function toggleMeni(Meni, ItemType)
{
  if (GetElement(Meni + '_Container').style.display == 'none')
  {
    GetElement(Meni + '_Container').style.display = 'block';
    GetElement(Meni).className = ItemType + 'collapse';
  }
  else
  {
    GetElement(Meni + '_Container').style.display = 'none';
    GetElement(Meni).className = ItemType + 'expand';
  }
  event.cancelBubble = true;
}

  function doIsci(elem, e)
  {

   {
     charCode = e.which;
   }
   else if (window.event)
   {
     e = window.event;
     charCode = e.keyCode;
   }
   if(charCode == 13)
   {
     document.location.href='/Stave/StavnaLista.aspx?search=' + elem.value
     return false
   }
  }
  function keyIsci()
  {
  elem = GetElement('ctl12_Modul5631_EditIskalecStav');
  if (elem.value != '')
    document.location.href='/Stave/StavnaLista.aspx?search=' + elem.value
  }

<script type='text/javascript'>
function showDocument(docId)
{
  if (GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).style.display == 'block')
    GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).style.display = 'none'
  else
  {
    if (GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).innerHTML == '')
      getDocumentData(docId);
    else
      GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).style.display = 'block'
  }
}
function getDocumentData(docId)
{
  var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function()
  {
    if(xmlhttp.readyState==4)
    { 
      var jHTML = eval('('+ xmlhttp.responseText +')'); 
      GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).innerHTML = jHTML.html;
      GetElement('documentDetail' + docId).style.display = 'block'
    }
  }
  if (xmlhttp != null)
  {
    xmlhttp.open('GET', '/_AjaxLoad.aspx?action=getDocument&CSRFToken=MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh&docID=' + docId, true);
    xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
    xmlhttp.send(null);
  }
}

<script language='javascript'>function formatNumber(num, decimals){	cNumN = '';	cNumD = '';	iLen = 0;	iLenN = 0;	cNum = num.toString()	iIndex = cNum .indexOf('.');	if (iIndex != -1)		cNumD = cNum.substr(iIndex + 1, cNum.length - iIndex);	iIndex = cNum.indexOf('.');	if (iIndex == -1)		iIndex = cNum.length + 1	cNum = cNum.substr(0, iIndex);	iLen = cNum.length;	while (iLen > 0)	{		cNumN = cNum.substr(iLen-1, 1) + cNumN;		iLenN = iLenN + 1;		if ((iLenN % 3 == 0) && (iLenN != cNum.length))			cNumN = '.' + cNumN;		iLen = iLen - 1;	}	if ((decimals > 0) && (cNumD.length < decimals))	{		for (i = 0; cNumD.length < decimals; i++)			cNumD = cNumD + '0';	}	if ((decimals > 0) && (cNumD.length > decimals))		cNumD = cNumD.substr(0, decimals);	if ((decimals > 0) && (cNumD != ''))		cNumN = cNumN + ',' + cNumD;	return cNumN;} </script><script language='javascript'>function Sgn(Number){  if (Number == 0)    return 0  else if (Number < 0)    return -1  else     return 1} </script><script language='javascript'>function Zaokrozi(aValue, aRound){  tRetValue = Math.floor(aValue* Math.pow(10, aRound) + Sgn(aValue) * 0.50000001);  tRetValue = tRetValue / Math.pow(10, aRound);  return tRetValue;} </script><script type='text/javascript'>

var beckTypes = '';
function setStavneMoznosti(betType, betSport, betOrder, pageNo)
{
  detailBack = '';
  beckTypes = '';
  var urlParams = '';
  var showfavorites = (GetElement('chShowFavorites') ? GetElement('chShowFavorites').checked : false);
  if (betSport == null) betSport = GetElement('_cbBetSport').value;
  if (betOrder == null) betOrder = GetElement('_cbBetOrder').value;
  if (pageNo == null) pageNo = 1;
  if (betType != null)
  {
    urlParams = betType;
  }
  else
  {
    var theForm = document.forms[0].elements['betOptions'];
    if (theForm.length == undefined)
      urlParams = theForm.value;
    else
    {
      for(i=0; i<theForm.length; i++)
      {
        if ((theForm[i].type == 'checkbox') && (theForm[i].checked))
        {
          if (urlParams != '') urlParams += ','; urlParams += theForm[i].value;
          beckTypes += '#' + theForm[i].value + '#';
        }
      }
    }
  }
  if (urlParams == '')
  {
      showAlert('Napaka', 'Izbrana mora biti vsaj ena stavna možnost!');
      return;
  }
  var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function()
  {
    if(xmlhttp.readyState==4)
    { 
      var jHTML = eval('('+ xmlhttp.responseText +')'); 
      if (jHTML.error != '')
        showAlert('Napaka', jHTML.error)
      else
        var myHash = Number(new Date());
        addHistory(myHash);
        GetElement('divBets').innerHTML = jHTML.html;
    }
  }
  if (xmlhttp != null)
  {
    GetElement('divBets').innerHTML = ''
    xmlhttp.open('GET', '/_BetList.aspx?action=addBetType&betHistory=' + historyHash + '&showfavorites=' + showfavorites.toString() + '&betSport=' + betSport + '&betOrder=' + betOrder + '&betTypes=' + urlParams + '&pageNo=' + pageNo + '&CSRFToken=MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh', true);
    xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
    xmlhttp.send(null);
  }
}
function natisniListo(date, league)
{
  var betTypes = '';
  var theForm = document.forms[0].elements['betOptions'];
  if ((theForm.type == 'checkbox') && (theForm.checked))
  {
              if (betTypes != '') betTypes += ','; betTypes += theForm.value;
  }
  else
  {
      for(i=0; i<theForm.length; i++)
      {
          if ((theForm[i].type == 'checkbox') && (theForm[i].checked))
          {
              if (betTypes != '') betTypes += ','; betTypes += theForm[i].value;
          }
      }
  }
  betSport = GetElement('_cbBetSport').value;
  strParams = '?VRI=' + betSport
  if (date != null) strParams += '&datOD=' + date;
  if (date != null) strParams += '&datDO=' + date;
  if (betTypes != null) strParams += '&PGT=' + betTypes;
  if (league != null) strParams += '&Selection=' + league;
  windowOpen(null, 'IzpisPonudbe', '/stave/Izpis.aspx' + strParams, 800, 600, 'status=0,toolbar=0,location=0,menubar=1,resizable=1,scrollbars=1');
}
function chShowFavoritesClick() {
  if (GetElement('chShowFavorites') != null && GetElement('lbShowFavorites') != null) {
    GetElement('chShowFavorites').checked = !GetElement('chShowFavorites').checked;
    if (GetElement('chShowFavorites').checked) {
      GetElement('lbShowFavorites').innerHTML = '<span class="icon-star fav-color"></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">Skrij izbor</span>';
    } else {
      GetElement('lbShowFavorites').innerHTML = '<span class="icon-star-empty fav-color"></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">Prikaži izbor</span>';
    }
  } else {
    console.error('Elements chShowFavorites or lbShowFavorites are not available!');
  }
  setStavneMoznosti();
}

<script type='text/javascript'>
function showAlert(title, message, mtype)
{
  if (mtype == null) mtype = 'error';
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_LabelAlertTitle').innerHTML = title;
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_LabelAlertMsg').innerHTML = message;
  var cvr = GetElement('coverDiv');
  var dlg = GetElement('alertDlg');
  if (mtype == 'error' || mtype == '')
  {
    dlg.className  = 'alertDialog';
    GetElement('alertIcon').src = '/images/icn_alert.gif';
    GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_alertLeft').className = 'alertLeft';
    GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_alertBody').className = 'alertBody';
    GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_alertTitle').className = 'alertTitle';
  }
  else if (mtype == 'info')
  {
    dlg.className  = 'infoDialog';
    GetElement('alertIcon').src = '/images/icn_alertOK.gif';
  }
  iShowPopUp('alertDlg', 'coverDiv');
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPotrdi').focus();
}
function closeAlertPopUp()
{
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPreklici').style.display = 'none';
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPreklici').href =  'javascript:void closeAlertPopUp();'
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPotrdi').href =  'javascript:void closeAlertPopUp();'
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPreklici').innerHTML = 'Prekliči';
  GetElement('ctl12_Alert1_btnPotrdi').innerHTML = 'V redu';
  iClosePopUp('alertDlg', 'coverDiv');
}

                    var timerOdgovornoIgranje;
                    var counterOdgovornoIgranje = 1;

                    function prikaziOdgovornoIgranje()
                    {
                        window.clearTimeout(timerOdgovornoIgranje)
                        //Prijava_IsLoggedInCallback(Prijava_IsLoggedIn_Success, Prijava_IsLoggedIn_Error)
                        Prijava_StartOdgovornoIgranjeCallback(Prijava_StartOdgovornoIgranjeCallback_Success, Prijava_StartOdgovornoIgranjeCallback_Error)
                    }

                    function startOdgovornoIgranje(interval)
                    {
                        if (timerOdgovornoIgranje != null) 
                            window.clearTimeout(timerOdgovornoIgranje)
                        timerOdgovornoIgranje = setTimeout(prikaziOdgovornoIgranje, interval)
                    }
                
                    function Prijava_StartOdgovornoIgranjeCallback_Success(result)
                    {
                        if (result == 'True')
                        {
                            var strMsg = 'Igrate že %s minut.\n\nBodite zmerni in igrajte predvsem za zabavo.';
                            if (typeof(showAlert) == 'function') 
                                showAlert('Opozorilo', strMsg.replace('%s', (60 * counterOdgovornoIgranje).toString()));
                            counterOdgovornoIgranje++;    startOdgovornoIgranje(3600000);

                        }
                   }

                   function Prijava_StartOdgovornoIgranjeCallback_Error(error)
                   {
                   }

                </script>

function doBack()
{
  if (detailBack != '')
  {
    GetElement('divBetList').innerHTML = detailBack;
    detailBack = '';
    var theForm = document.forms[0].elements['betOptions'];
    if (theForm != undefined)
    {
      for(i=0; i<theForm.length; i++)
      {
        if (beckTypes.indexOf('#' + theForm[i].value + '#') != -1)
        {
          theForm[i].checked = true;
        }
      }
    }
    return;
  }
  var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function()
  {
    if(xmlhttp.readyState==4)
    { 
      var jHTML = eval('('+ xmlhttp.responseText +')'); 
      if (jHTML.error != '')
        showAlert('Napaka', jHTML.error)
      else
      {
        GetElement('divBetList').innerHTML = jHTML.html;
        if (jHTML.script != '')
          eval(jHTML.script);
      }
    }
  }
  if (xmlhttp != null)
  {
    xmlhttp.open('GET', '/_BetList.aspx?action=doBack&betHistory=' + historyHash + '&CSRFToken=MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh', true);
    xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
    xmlhttp.send(null);
  }
}

var detailBack = ''
function eventDetail(eventId, ajaxDetail)
{
  detailBack = '';
  if (ajaxDetail == true)
  {
    var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
    xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=function()
    {
      if(xmlhttp.readyState==4)
      { 
        var jHTML = eval('('+ xmlhttp.responseText +')'); 
        if (jHTML.error != '')
          showAlert('Napaka', jHTML.error)
        else
        {
          var myHash = Number(new Date());
          addHistory(myHash);
          detailBack = GetElement('divBetList').innerHTML;
          GetElement('divBetList').innerHTML = jHTML.html;
          window.scrollTo(0,0);
        }
      }
    }
    if (xmlhttp != null)
    {
      xmlhttp.open('GET', '/_BetList.aspx?action=eventDetail&betHistory=' + historyHash + '&eventId=' + eventId + '&CSRFToken=MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh', true);
      xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
      xmlhttp.send(null);
    }
  }
  else
  {
    document.location.href='/Stave/StavnaLista.aspx?eventId=' + eventId
  }
}
function hideBetListBlock(id)
{
  GetElement(id).style.display = 'none';
}
function OznaciStavo(listId, eventId, typeId, add)
{
  var linki = document.getElementsByTagName('a');
  for(i=0; i<linki.length; i++)
  {
    if (linki[i].id == 'stava' + listId + '_' + eventId + '_' + typeId)
    {
      if (add == 1)
        linki[i].className = 'btn selected';
      else
        linki[i].className = 'btn yellow';
    }
  }
  if (GetElement('ts_stava' + listId + '_' + eventId + '_' + typeId) != null)
  {
    if (add == 1)
      GetElement('ts_stava' + listId + '_' + eventId + '_' + typeId).className = 'btn selected';
    else
      GetElement('ts_stava' + listId + '_' + eventId + '_' + typeId).className = 'btn yellow';
  }
}
function addBetList(listId, eventId, typeId, topStave)
{
  var add = 1;
  if (GetElement(topStave + 'stava' + listId + '_' + eventId + '_' + typeId).className=='btn selected')
    add = 0;
  if (add==1) actionId = 'addBet'; else actionId = 'removeBet';
  if (typeof(addBet) == 'function') addBet(actionId, listId, eventId, typeId, add);
}
function setFavorite(adding, id, tip, callback)
{
  var actionId = adding ? 'addFavorites' : 'removeFavorites';
  var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
  xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function()
  {
    if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4)
    { 
      var jHTML = eval('('+ xmlhttp.responseText +')'); 
      if (jHTML.error != '')
        showAlert('Napaka', jHTML.error)
      else
      {
        if (typeof callback === 'function') callback();      }
    }
  }
  if (xmlhttp != null)
  {
    xmlhttp.open('GET', '/_AjaxLoad.aspx?action=' + actionId + '&id=' + id + '&tip=' + tip + '&CSRFToken=MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh', true);
    xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
    xmlhttp.send(null);
  }
}
function setFavoritePrireditev(id, tip)
{
  var adding = GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).src.indexOf('/images/icn_my_profile_panel_add.gif') != -1;
  setFavorite(adding, id, tip, function callback()
  {
    if (adding)
    {
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).src = GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).src.replace('/images/icn_my_profile_panel_add.gif', '/images/icn_my_profile_panel_remove.gif')
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).alt = 'Odstrani iz mojega izbora'
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).title = 'Odstrani iz mojega izbora'
    }
    else
    {
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).src = GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).src.replace('/images/icn_my_profile_panel_remove.gif', '/images/icn_my_profile_panel_add.gif')
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).alt = 'Dodaj v moj izbor'
      GetElement('imgFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).title = 'Dodaj v moj izbor'
    }
  });
}
function setFavoriteEkipa(id, tip)
{
  var adding = GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).className.indexOf('icon-star-empty') !== -1;
  setFavorite(adding, id, tip, function callback()
  {
    if (adding)
    {
      GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).className = GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).className.replace('icon-star-empty', 'icon-star');
      GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).title = 'Odstrani iz mojega izbora';
    }
    else
    {
      GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).className = GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).className.replace('icon-star', 'icon-star-empty');
      GetElement('iconFavorite' + id + '-' + tip).title = 'Dodaj v moj izbor';
    }
  });
}

    $(document).ready(function () {

    function PotrdiPiskotke()
    {
        var exdate = new Date();
        exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + 10000);
        var c_value = escape("1") + ";expires=" + exdate.toUTCString() + ";path=/;";
        document.cookie = "NastavitvePiskotkov" + "=" + c_value;
    }

<script>
    var kosPopUp;

    function odpriKosaricoPopup() {
        if (kosPopUp && kosPopUp.isOpen)
            return;

         kosPopUp = new jBox('Modal', {
            id: 'kosPopUp',
            fixed: false,
            reposition: true,
            repositionOnOpen:true,
            attach: $('#btnKosPopup'),
            target: $('#btnKosPopup'),
            position: {
                x: getLeft($('#btnKosPopup')[0]) - 320 + $('#btnKosPopup').width()+20,
                y: getTop($('#btnKosPopup')[0]) + $('#btnKosPopup').height()+20,
            },
            outside: 'y',
            zIndex: 900000,
            width: 320,
            //height: 500,
            content: $('#ctl12_KosaricaPopUp1_Kosarica1'),
            overlay: false,
            blockScroll: false,
            
            ajax: {
                url: '/_Ajax_kosarica.aspx',
                data: 'RCE_TIP=-1',
                reload: true,
                cache: false,
                complete: function()
                {
                    setScrollerKosarica();
                }
                
            },
            onCloseComplete: function(){
                kosPopUp.destroy();
            }
        });
        kosPopUp.open();
    }

    function updateKosBtn(cnt)
    {
        var kosBadge = $("#kos_badge");
        if (cnt > 0 && kosBadge.length == 0) {
            kosBadge = $("<div/>", {
                class: "badge",
                id: "kos_badge",
            }).appendTo("#btnKosPopup").text(cnt);
        }
        else if (cnt == 0 && kosBadge.length > 0)
            kosBadge.detach();
        else
            kosBadge.text(cnt);

    }
    
    function notifyKosarica(text)
    {
        var content = text || 'Listek je bil dodan v košarico!';
       

        var tooltip = new jBox('Tooltip', {
            content: content,
            reposition: true,
            repositionOnOpen:true,
                zIndex: 900000,
            position: {
                x: getLeft($('#btnKosPopup')[0]) - 200 + $('#btnKosPopup').width()+20,
                y: getTop($('#btnKosPopup')[0]) + $('#btnKosPopup').height(),
            },
            //pointer: 'center',
            pointTo:'top',
            pointer: 'left:' + (200 - $('#btnKosPopup').width() - ($('#btnKosPopup').width()/2)).toString(),
            theme: 'TooltipDark',
            autoClose: 3000,
            target: $("#btnKosPopup"),
            outside: 'y',
            
        });
        tooltip.open();
        setTimeout(function () { tooltip.close() }, 3000);


        //reload vsebine, če je odprt popup
        if (kosPopUp && kosPopUp.isOpen)
            kosPopUp.open();
        
    }
    function setScrollerKosarica() {
       
        var kos = $('.jBox-content > .div_Kosarica > .div_Kosarica');
        if (kos.length == 0)
            kos = $('.jBox-content > .div_Kosarica');
        if (!kos.mCustomScrollbar) //ni skripta za scrolling!
            return;

        kos.css('max-height', '500px');

        kos.mCustomScrollbar({
            theme: 'dark-thin',
            scrollInertia: 500,

        });
        $('.scroller .padding').css('padding-right', 0);
        $('.mCSB_inside > .mCSB_container').css('margin-right', 15);
        
    }
</script>

<script>
    $(window).load(function () {
        Kosarica_getCount();
    });

    function Kosarica_getCount()
    {
        try{
            Kosarica_GetCountCallback(Kosarica_GetCountCallbackSuccess, Kosarica_GetCountCallbackFailure);
        }
        catch(e)
        {

        }
    }

    function Kosarica_GetCountCallbackSuccess(result)
    {
        if (updateKosBtn && result > 0)
            updateKosBtn(result);

    }

    function Kosarica_GetCountCallbackFailure()
    {
        console.error("Error: Kosarica_getCount;");
    }

    function AkcijaKosarica(akcija, id, vs) {
        betValue = '';

        if ($("#betValue").length)
            betValue = $("#betValue").val();

        $("img.kosarica_loading").show();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/_BetSlip.aspx',
            data: {
                action: akcija,
                listId: id,
                vs: vs,
                betValue: betValue,
                CSRFToken: strCSRFToken,
            },

            cache: false,
        }).done(function (data, status, jqXHR) {
            var jHTML = eval('(' + data + ')');
            
            if (jHTML.error != '')
                showAlert(strNapaka, jHTML.error);
            else
            {
                if (akcija != 'checkBasket') {
                    $('div.div_Kosarica').html(jHTML.html);
                   
                    if (setScrollerKosarica)
                        setScrollerKosarica();
                }
            }
                

            if (jHTML.script != '')
                eval(jHTML.script);
        })
        .always(function () {
            $("img.kosarica_loading").hide();
            AkcijaOsveziListek();
        });
    }

    function NaloziKosarico(el, vs) {
        
        var input = $(el).closest('div.div_Kosarica').find("input#EditKosarica");
        
        AkcijaKosarica("loadBasket", input.val(), vs);
    }

    function AkcijaOsveziListek() {
        
        $.ajax({
            url: '/_BetSlip.aspx',
            data: {
                action: 'refreshBetSlip',
                CSRFToken: strCSRFToken,
            },

            cache: false,
        }).done(function (data, status, jqXHR) {
            var jHTML = eval('(' + data + ')');

            if (jHTML.error != '')
                showAlert(strNapaka, jHTML.error);
            else {
                $('#divBetSlip').html(jHTML.html);
            }

            if (jHTML.script != '')
                eval(jHTML.script);
        });
    }
</script>

<script>
    var strCSRFToken = "MjM2YTA3NjMtOTQyYy00NTUyLWEyYTctZTNhMTQzMmU0MWRh";

    function KontrolaSeje()
    {
        try{
            KontrolaSejeCallback(KontrolaSeje_success, KontrolaSeje_err, strCSRFToken);
        }
        catch(e)
        {
            console.error(e.message);
        }
    }

    function KontrolaSeje_success(result)
    {
        var JSON = eval('('+result+')');

        if (!JSON.validSession)
        {
            location.href = '/?sessiontimeout=true';
        }
        else
        {
            setTimeout(KontrolaSeje, (1*60*1000)); //potem preverjamo na minuto
        }
    }
    
    function KontrolaSeje_err(error)
    {
        if (error.get_exceptionType() == "iPLUS.Web.UI.CSRFTokenException")
            location.href = '/?sessiontimeout=true';
    }

</script>

    <div id='ctl12_Modul5634_PanelListek_Panel' class='cPanel'><div class='cPanelHeader'><div class='cPanelHeaderTXT'><h1>Stavni listek</h1></div><div id='ctl12_Modul5634_PanelListek_SelekcijaArrow' class='cPanelArrowContractBTN' onclick='toggleSelekcija("ctl12_Modul5634_PanelListek_SelekcijaContent", "ctl12_Modul5634_PanelListek_SelekcijaArrow","cPanelArrowExpandBTN","cPanelArrowContractBTN")'></div></div><div id='ctl12_Modul5634_PanelListek_SelekcijaContent' class='cPanelContent grey'>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var inputVZD = false;
    var prebitekVZD = false;

    var betInput_nacin = 1;  
    var betInput_vrednost = 0;

    function potrdiStavo()
    {
        if (GetElement('betValue') != null)
        {
            if (GetElement('betValue').value == '')
            {
                betInput_vrednost = 0;
                var minVpl;
                var stKomb = SteviloKombinacij();
                if (stKomb > 1)
                    minVpl = formatNumber(Zaokrozi(stKomb * (PAR_MKS * (100 + DAV_SDV) / 100),2),2);
                else
                    minVpl = formatNumber(Zaokrozi(PON_MIZ * (100 + DAV_SDV) / 100,2),2);
                showAlert(strNAPAKA, 'Za vplačilo listka je potrebno vnesti znesek plačila. Minimalno plačilo je <'+ minVpl +'>');
                return;
            }
        }
        addBet('checkBet', 0, 0, '1', 0);
    }

    function potrdiKosarico()
    {
        addBet('addBasket', 0, 0, '', 0);
    }

    function addFromBetSlip(elemId)
    {
        if (GetElement(elemId).value != "")
        {
            addBet('addFromBetSlip', GetElement(elemId).value, 0, '', 0);
        }
    }

    function selectBasket()
    {
        if (GetElement('imKosarica') == null)
            return;
        if (GetElement('imKosarica').src.indexOf('/images/icn_check.gif') != -1)
            GetElement('imKosarica').src = GetElement('imKosarica').src.replace('icn_check.gif', 'icn_uncheck.gif');
        else
            GetElement('imKosarica').src = GetElement('imKosarica').src.replace('icn_uncheck.gif', 'icn_check.gif')
    }

    function loadBasket(elemId)
    {
        if (GetElement(elemId).value != "")
        {
            addBet('loadBasket', GetElement(elemId).value, 0, '', 0);
        }
    }

    function setBetSystem()
    {
        addBet('setBetSystem', GetElement('betSystem').value, 0, '', 0);
    }


    function setBetVZD()
    {
        bZNSChanged = true;

        //shranimo izbor;
        if (GetElement('cbVZD'))
            inputVZD = GetElement('cbVZD').checked;
   
        addBet('setBetVZD', 0, 0, '', 0, null,  (GetElement('cbVZD') !== null ? GetElement('cbVZD').checked : false));                                          
    }

    function PreracunajMaxVplacilo(MaxZnesek)
    {
        var maxKvota = 0;
        
        if (GetElement('cbVZD') !== null && GetElement('cbVZD').checked)
        {
    
            /*
                en zgrešen - izračunamo vplačilo na glavno kombinacijo
            */

            for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++) {
                if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD != '1') {
                    maxKvota = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3;
                }
            }
            NoviZnesek = MaxZnesek / maxKvota;

        }
        else           
        {
            
            for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
            {
                maxKvota = maxKvota + arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK;              
            }
            maxKvota = maxKvota * arrayKombinacije[0].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[0].SLF_FAK3; 
            NoviZnesek = MaxZnesek;
            NoviZnesek = NoviZnesek / maxKvota;
        }


        NoviZnesek = NoviZnesek * (1/(1 - PAR_AST / 100))
        if (PAR_RND != 0)
        {
            NoviZnesek = Math.floor(NoviZnesek * Math.pow(10, PAR_RND));
            NoviZnesek = Zaokrozi(NoviZnesek / Math.pow(10, PAR_RND), 2);
        }
        else
            NoviZnesek = Math.floor(NoviZnesek);


        if (GetElement('cbVZD') !== null && GetElement('cbVZD').checked)
        {
            /*
                en zgrešen - izračunamo skupno vplačilo
            */
            SLG_ZNS = NoviZnesek;  // uporabim v funkciji NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo()
            prebitekVZD = false;    // nastavim v funkciji NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo()
            NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo();

            if (prebitekVZD)
            {
                // način, če uporabimo minimalno vplačilo na kombinacijo

                var sumSLG_BDBK = 0;
                var sumSLG_ZNS = 0;
                var dblFAK = 1;

                for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++) {
                    if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD == '1') {

                        sumSLG_BDBK += arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB;
                        sumSLG_ZNS += arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS;

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        //kvota glavne kombinacije
                        dblFAK = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3;
                    }
                }

                NoviZnesek = (MaxZnesek - (sumSLG_BDBK)) / dblFAK + sumSLG_ZNS;

            }
            else
            {
                // (star) način - če uporabimo vplačilo za dobitek VZD kombinacij

                var tmpFaktor = 1;

                for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++) {
                    if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD == '1') {
                        tmpFaktor -= 1 / (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3);
                    }
                    else {
                        maxKvota = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3;
                    }
                }

                // VPL = DOB / (st.komb-1 + FAKk * (1-1/FAK1-1/FAK2-...)) 
                NoviZnesek = MaxZnesek / (arrayKombinacije.length - 1 + maxKvota * tmpFaktor);
            }

            NoviZnesek = NoviZnesek * (1 / (1 - PAR_AST / 100))
            if (PAR_RND != 0) {
                NoviZnesek = Math.floor(NoviZnesek * Math.pow(10, PAR_RND));
                NoviZnesek = Zaokrozi(NoviZnesek / Math.pow(10, PAR_RND), 2);
            }
            else
                NoviZnesek = Math.floor(NoviZnesek);

        }
        
        return NoviZnesek;
    }

    function SteviloKombinacij()
    {
        var iCnt = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD != '1')
                iCnt++;
        }
        return iCnt;
    }

    function NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo()
    {
        var SLG_ZNS_VZD = 0;
        var kombMaxKvota = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD == '1')
            {
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS/(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3), 6);
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDBO = SLG_ZNS;
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB = SLG_ZNS;
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_BDB1 = SLG_ZNS;
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_DAV = 0;

                if (kombMaxKvota == null || kombMaxKvota.SLG_FAK < arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK)
                    kombMaxKvota = arrayKombinacije[i];
                                                    
                SLG_ZNS_VZD += arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS;
            }
                                                
        }

        if (kombMaxKvota != null && kombMaxKvota.SLG_ZNS < SLG_EZVK)
        {   
            var dblSLG_BDBK = Zaokrozi(kombMaxKvota.SLG_FAK *  kombMaxKvota.SLF_FAK2 * kombMaxKvota.SLF_FAK3 * SLG_EZVK, 2);
            SLG_ZNS_VZD = 0;

            prebitekVZD = true;

            for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
            {
                if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD == '1')
                {
                    arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(dblSLG_BDBK / (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 * arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3), 6);
                    arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDBO = dblSLG_BDBK;
                    arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB = dblSLG_BDBK;
                    arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_BDB1 = dblSLG_BDBK;
                    arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_DAV = 0;
                                                    
                    SLG_ZNS_VZD += arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS;
                }
                                                
            }
            SLG_ZNS_VZD = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS_VZD, 6);
            

        }

        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD != '1')
            {
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS =  Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS - SLG_ZNS_VZD,6);
            }
        }

        return ((SLG_ZNS - SLG_ZNS_VZD) > 0);
    }

    function Dobitek_OnChange()
    {
        betInput_nacin = 3;
        
        betInput_vrednost = GetElement('betPrize').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.');
        if (isNaN(betInput_vrednost))
            betInput_vrednost = 0;

        //console.log("Dobitek_OnChange nacin:" + betInput_nacin.toString() + ' vred: ' + betInput_vrednost);

    }

    function Placilo_OnChange()
    {
        
        betInput_nacin = 1;

        betInput_vrednost = GetElement('betSumValue').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.');
        if (isNaN(betInput_vrednost))
            betInput_vrednost = 0;

    }

    function PreracunajDobitek(showSum, showBetPrize, silent, minVplKontrola)
    {
        
        silent = silent || false;
        minVplKontrola = minVplKontrola || false;

        //console.log('vpl: ' + GetElement('betSumValue').value);
        
        if (GetElement('betValue') == null || GetElement('betValue') == '')
            return;

        //Dolocimo ZNS
        if (isNaN(GetElement('betValue').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.')))
            SLG_ZNS = 0; 
        else 
            SLG_ZNS = GetElement('betValue').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.'); 
        if (SLG_ZNS != 0)
        {
            if (SLG_ZNS != Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2))
                GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(SLG_ZNS, 2);
        }
        SLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2);
        
        if (GetElement('betSumValue') !== document.activeElement && GetElement('betPrize') !== document.activeElement) {
            //če ne vpisujemo več vrednosti in ni možen za VZD, izklopimo VZD še serverside
            if (GetElement('cbVZD') && inputVZD === true && GetElement('cbVZD').checked !== inputVZD)
            {
                DolociVplacilo(true);
                setBetVZD();
                return;                        
            }

        }
        
        var stKomb = SteviloKombinacij();
        //pribitki
        PreracunajPribitekKvoto(SLG_ZNS);
                                        
        if (!NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo() && GetElement('cbVZD') !== null && GetElement('cbVZD').checked)
        {
            //ni veljaven za vzd
            if (GetElement('betSumValue') === document.activeElement || GetElement('betPrize') === document.activeElement )
            {
                //če še vpisujemo vrednosti in še ni veljaven, ne računamo
                GetElement('cbVZD').checked = false;
                GetElement('betValue').value = 0;
                SLG_ZNS = 0;
                NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo();
            }
            else
            {
                GetElement('cbVZD').checked = false;
                setBetVZD();

                if (!silent)
                    showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi prenizke kvote opcija zgrešen dogodek ni možna!'); 
                return;
            }
        }
        else if (GetElement('cbVZD') !== null && !GetElement('cbVZD').checked && inputVZD)
        {
            //če je postal spet veljaven za VZD, ga vklopimo    
            if (GetElement('betSumValue') === document.activeElement)
            {
                GetElement('cbVZD').checked = true;
                DolociVplacilo();               
            }
            else if (GetElement('betPrize') === document.activeElement)
            {
                GetElement('cbVZD').checked = true;
                DolociVplaciloIzIzplacila();
            }
            else
            {
                inputVZD = false;
            }
                
            return;

        }

        var maxSLG_ZNS = 0;
        var sumSLG_ZNS = 0;
                                            
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            if ((arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS) > maxSLG_ZNS)
            {
                maxSLG_ZNS = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3;
            }
            sumSLG_ZNS += arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK * arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3;
        }
        
        /*
        console.log("SLG_ZNS: " + SLG_ZNS);
        console.log("maxSLG_ZNS: " + maxSLG_ZNS);
        console.log("sumSLG_ZNS: " + sumSLG_ZNS);
        console.trace();
        console.log("--------------------------");
        */
        
        if (((maxSLG_ZNS > PON_MZI) || (stKomb > 1 && sumSLG_ZNS > PAR_MDS) || (GetElement('cbVZD') && GetElement('cbVZD').checked && (sumSLG_ZNS > PON_MZI)))
            && (GetElement('betSumValue') !== document.activeElement && GetElement('betPrize') !== document.activeElement ))
        {

            if (stKomb > 1)
                NoviZnesek = PreracunajMaxVplacilo(PAR_MDS);
            else
                NoviZnesek = PreracunajMaxVplacilo(PON_MZI);

            var vpl = NoviZnesek;
            if (stKomb > 1)
                vpl = vpl * stKomb;
            /*
            console.log("NoviZnesek: " + NoviZnesek);
            console.log("vpl: " + vpl);
            */
            
            if (vpl > PON_MZI)
            {
                SLG_ZNS = 0;
                GetElement('betValue').value = '';
                betInput_vrednost = 0;

                if (!silent)
                    showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi previsoke kvote stave ni možno sprejeti!');
            }
            else
            {
                if (vpl < PON_MIZ || minVplKontrola)
                {
                    SLG_ZNS = 0;
                    GetElement('betValue').value = '';
                    betInput_vrednost = 0;

                    if (!silent)
                        showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi previsoke kvote stave ni možno sprejeti!');
                }
                else
                {
                    SLG_ZNS = NoviZnesek;
                    
                    GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(SLG_ZNS, 2);

                    /*if (stKomb > 1)
                        betInput_vrednost = PAR_MDS;
                    else
                        betInput_vrednost = PON_MZI;
                        */
                    betInput_vrednost = 0;

                    betInput_nacin = 3;
                    
                    if (!silent)
                        showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi previsoke kvote je bil zmanjšan znesek za plačilo!'); 
                }
            }
            NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo();

        }
        
        

        if (SLG_ZNS != Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2))
        {
            SLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2); 
        }

        //kontrola minimalno vplačilo

        if (!minVplKontrola && (GetElement('betSumValue') !== document.activeElement && GetElement('betPrize') !== document.activeElement)) {
            var vpl = SLG_ZNS;

            if (stKomb > 1) {
                if (vpl < PAR_MKS) {
                    //console.error("vpl < PAR_MKS");
                    SLG_ZNS = PAR_MKS;
                    GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(PAR_MKS, 2);
                    betInput_vrednost = 0;
                    /*
                    var minVpl = Zaokrozi(stKomb * (PAR_MKS * (100 + DAV_SDV) / 100), 2);

                    betInput_vrednost = minVpl;
                    betInput_nacin = 1;
                    */
                    NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo();
                    
                    if (!silent)
                        showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi prenizkega vplačila na kombinacijo je bil znesek za plačilo povečan!');
                    PreracunajDobitek(showSum, showBetPrize, silent, true);
                    return;

                }
                vpl = Zaokrozi(vpl * stKomb, 2);
            }

            if (vpl < PON_MIZ) {
                //console.error("vpl < PAR_MKS");
                SLG_ZNS = PON_MIZ;
                GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(PON_MIZ, 2);
                betInput_vrednost = 0;
                /*
                var minVpl = Zaokrozi(PON_MIZ * (100 + DAV_SDV) / 100, 2);

                betInput_vrednost = minVpl;
                betInput_nacin = 1;
                */

                NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo();
                
                if (!silent)
                    showAlert(strOPOZORILO, 'Zaradi prenizkega vplačila na kombinacijo je bil znesek za plačilo povečan!');
                PreracunajDobitek(showSum, showBetPrize, silent, true);
                return;
            }
        }
        

       

        if (GetElement('divListekZaIzplaciloEnZgresen'))
            GetElement('divListekZaIzplaciloEnZgresen').style.display = 'none';

        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {

            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_VZD == '1' )
            {
                // vrednosti kombinacij VZD se nastavijo v NastaviVplaciloNaKombinacijo
                if (GetElement('cbVZD') && GetElement('cbVZD').checked && SLG_ZNS > 0)
                {
                    GetElement('divListekZaIzplaciloEnZgresen').style.display = '';
                    GetElement('betPayOutEnZgresen').innerHTML = formatNumber(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB, 2); 
                }
            
            }                

            var SLG_FAKO = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAKO;
            var SLG_FAK = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK;
            var SLG_DAV = 0;
            var SLG_IZP = 0;
            var SLG_BDBO = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS * SLG_FAKO, 2);
            var SLF_BDB1 = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS * SLG_FAK, 2);
            var SLG_BDB = SLF_BDB1;
            var SLF_ZNS3 = 0
            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 > 1.00)
                SLF_ZNS3 = Zaokrozi((arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 - 1.00) * Zaokrozi(SLF_BDB1, 2), 2);
            if (arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 > 1.00) {
                SLG_BDB = Zaokrozi(Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB, 2) + SLF_ZNS3, 2);
            }
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDBO = SLG_BDBO;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB = SLG_BDB;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_DAV = SLG_DAV;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_BDB1 = SLF_BDB1;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3 = SLF_ZNS3;
                
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            var SLF_ZNS2 = 0
            var SLG_DAV = 0
            var SLG_BDB = arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB
            if(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 > 1.00) 
                SLF_ZNS2 = Zaokrozi((arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 - 1.00) * Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB, 2), 2)
            if(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 > 1.00){ 
                SLG_BDB = Zaokrozi(Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB, 2) + SLF_ZNS2, 2)
            } 
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 = SLF_ZNS2;
            if (SLG_BDB > PDO_MDD)
            {SLG_DAV = Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB * PDO_SDD / 100, 2)}
            else
            {SLG_DAV = 0}
            SLG_IZP = Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB - SLG_DAV, PAR_RND)
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_IZP = SLG_IZP;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB = SLG_BDB;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_DAV = SLG_DAV;
        }
        SLG_BDBO = 0;
        SLG_BDB = 0;
        SLG_DAV = 0;
        SLG_IZP = 0;
        SLF_ZNS2 = 0;
        SLF_BDB1 = 0;
        SLF_ZNS3 = 0;
        SLF_FAK3 = 0;
        for(var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            SLG_BDBO += Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDBO, 2);
            SLG_DAV += Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_DAV, 2);
            SLF_ZNS2 += Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2, 2);
            SLF_BDB1 += Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_BDB1, 2);
            tSLF_ZNS3 = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3, 2);
            tSLG_BDB = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB, 2);
            tSLG_IZP = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_IZP, 2);
            if(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 > 1.0 && arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS > 0.00 && Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3, 2) < 0.01) 
            {
                SLF_ZNS3 += Zaokrozi(tSLF_ZNS3 + 0.01, 2);
                SLG_BDB += Zaokrozi(tSLG_BDB + 0.01, 2);
                SLG_IZP += Zaokrozi(tSLG_IZP + 0.01, 2);
            }
            else {
                SLF_ZNS3 += tSLF_ZNS3;
                SLG_BDB += tSLG_BDB;
                SLG_IZP += tSLG_IZP;
            }
        }

        SLF_BDB1 = Zaokrozi(SLF_BDB1 + SLF_ZNS3, 2); 
        SLG_BDB = Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB, 2);
        SLG_BDBO = Zaokrozi(SLG_BDBO, 2);
        SLG_IZP = Zaokrozi(SLG_IZP, 2);
        SLG_DAV = Zaokrozi(SLG_DAV, 2);

        SLG_DAVV = 0;
        if (DAV_SDV != 0)
        {
            if (SLG_ZNS > DAV_MZV)
                SLG_DAVV = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS * (DAV_SDV / 100), 2) * stKomb;
        }
        if ((showSum == true) && (GetElement('betSumValue') != null))
        {
            if (SLG_ZNS > 0)
                GetElement('betSumValue').value = formatNumber(Zaokrozi((SLG_ZNS * stKomb) + SLG_DAVV, 2), 2);
            else
                GetElement('betSumValue').value = '';
        }
        if (GetElement('betPrizeOld') != null)
            GetElement('betPrizeOld').innerHTML = formatNumber(SLG_BDBO, 2) + ' EUR';
        if (GetElement('betPrize') != null && showBetPrize) { 
            if (SLG_BDB > 0)
                GetElement('betPrize').value = formatNumber(SLG_BDB, 2);
            else
                GetElement('betPrize').value = '';
        }
        if (GetElement('betBonusVIP') != null) {
            if (SLG_BDB > 0)
                GetElement('betBonusVIP').innerHTML = '+' + formatNumber(Zaokrozi(SLG_BDB - SLG_BDBO, 2), 2);
            else
                GetElement('betBonusVIP').innerHTML = formatNumber(0, 2);
        }
        if (SLG_IZP > 0) {
            GetElement('betVat').innerHTML = formatNumber(SLG_DAV, 2);
            GetElement('betPayOut').innerHTML = formatNumber(SLG_IZP, 2);
        }
        else
        {
            GetElement('betVat').innerHTML = formatNumber(0, 2);
            GetElement('betPayOut').innerHTML = formatNumber(0, 2);
        }
        if (GetElement('betWinBase'))
        {
            if (SLG_BDBO > 0)
                GetElement('betWinBase').innerHTML = formatNumber(SLG_BDBO, 2);
            else
                GetElement('betWinBase').innerHTML = formatNumber(0, 2);
        }
        SkrijKontrole(SLG_DAV);
        if (GetElement('betBonusPribitek') != null) {
            if (SLF_ZNS2 > 0)
                GetElement('betBonusPribitek').innerHTML = formatNumber(SLF_ZNS2, 2) + ' EUR';
            else
                GetElement('betBonusPribitek').innerHTML = formatNumber(0, 2);
        }
        
    }

    function DolociVplacilo(brezPreracuna, event)
    {
        
        try {
            if (event) {
                var x = event.which || event.keyCode;
                //console.log("keycode: " +x);
                if (!(x >= 48 && x <= 57)
                    && !(x >= 96 && x <= 105)
                    && x != 188 //comma
                    && x != 190 //period
                    && x != 110  //decimal point (numpad)
                    && x != 8   //backspace
                    && x != 46   //delete
                    && x != 229   //mobile touch input
                    )
                {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        catch(e)
        {
            console.error('event.keykode!');
        }

        if (GetElement('betSumValue') != null)
        {
            lSLG_ZNS = GetElement('betSumValue').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.');
            if (isNaN(lSLG_ZNS)) {
                GetElement('betValue').value = '';
                betInput_vrednost = 0;
            }
            else {
                
                lSLG_ZNSZ = lSLG_ZNS;
                lSLG_DAVZ = 0;
                var stKomb = SteviloKombinacij();
                if (DAV_SDV != 0) {
                    lSLG_ZNSZ = Math.floor(lSLG_ZNSZ / stKomb * 100) / 100;
                    
                    lSLG_ZNSZ = Zaokrozi(lSLG_ZNSZ * 100.00 / (100.00 + DAV_SDV), 2);
                    lSLG_DAVZ = Zaokrozi(lSLG_ZNSZ * DAV_SDV / 100, 2);
                }
                if (Zaokrozi((lSLG_DAVZ * stKomb) +
                             (lSLG_ZNSZ * stKomb), 2) > Zaokrozi(lSLG_ZNS, 2)) {
                    
                    lSLG_ZNS = lSLG_ZNS * 100 / (100 + DAV_SDV);
                    lSLG_ZNS = Math.floor((lSLG_ZNS / stKomb) * 100) / 100;
                }
                else {
                    lSLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(lSLG_ZNSZ, 2);
                }

                if (lSLG_ZNS > 0)
                    GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(lSLG_ZNS, 2);
                else {
                    GetElement('betValue').value = '';
                    betInput_vrednost = 0;
                }

            }
            
            if (!brezPreracuna)
                PreracunajDobitek(false, true);
        }
    }

    

    function DolociVplaciloIzIzplacila(event)
    {
        try {
            if (event) {
                var x = event.which || event.keyCode;
                //console.log("keycode: " +x);
                if (!(x >= 48 && x <= 57)
                    && !(x >= 96 && x <= 105)
                    && x != 188 //comma
                    && x != 190 //period
                    && x != 110  //decimal point (numpad)
                    && x != 8   //backspace
                    && x != 46   //delete
                    && x != 229   //mobile touch input
                    )
                {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        catch (e) {
            console.error('event.keykode!');
        }

        if (GetElement('betPrize') != null)
        {
            SLG_BDB = parseFloat(GetElement('betPrize').value.replace('.', '').replace(',', '.'));
            if (isNaN(SLG_BDB))
            {
                SLG_BDB = 0;
                GetElement('betPrize').value = '';
            }
            if (SLG_BDB == 0)
            {
                GetElement('betValue').value = '';
                GetElement('betSumValue').value = '';
                betInput_vrednost = 0;
                return;
            }
            SLG_BDB = SLG_BDB + (49.9999 / (Math.pow(10, PAR_RND) * Math.pow(10, PAR_RND)));
            
            NoviZnesek = PreracunajMaxVplacilo(SLG_BDB);
            SLG_ZNS = NoviZnesek;

            GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(SLG_ZNS, 2);
        
            if (SLG_ZNS != Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2))
            {
                SLG_ZNS = Zaokrozi(SLG_ZNS, 2); 
            }
            GetElement('betValue').value = formatNumber(SLG_ZNS, 2); 
            PreracunajDobitek(true, false, false);
            
        }

    }

    function PreracunajPribitekKvoto(SLG_ZNS)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            var SLF_BDB1 = Zaokrozi(arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_ZNS * arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_FAK, 2);

            if(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 > 1.00)
            {
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 = Zaokrozi((arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 - 1.00) * SLF_BDB1, 2)
            }
            else{
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 = 0;
            }
            if(arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 > 1.00)
            {
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3 = Zaokrozi((arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 - 1.00) * SLF_BDB1, 2)
                                                  
            }
            else{
                arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3 = 0;
            }
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLG_BDB = SLF_BDB1 + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS2 + arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_ZNS3;
        }
    }

    function iKombinacija (Index, Komb, SLG_FAKO, SLG_FAK, SLG_BDBO, SLG_BDB, SLG_DAV, SLF_ZNS2, SLF_FAK2, SLF_BDB1, SLF_IZP, SLF_FAK3, SLF_ZNS3, SLG_ZNS, SLG_VZD)
    {
        this.Index = Index
        this.Komb = Komb
        this.SLG_FAKO = SLG_FAKO
        this.SLG_FAK = SLG_FAK
        this.SLG_BDBO = SLG_BDBO
        this.SLG_BDB = SLG_BDB
        this.SLG_DAV = SLG_DAV
        this.SLF_ZNS2 = SLF_ZNS2
        this.SLF_FAK2 = SLF_FAK2
        this.SLF_BDB1 = SLF_BDB1
        this.SLF_IZP = SLF_IZP
        this.SLF_ZNS3 = SLF_ZNS3
        this.SLF_FAK3 = SLF_FAK3
        this.SLG_ZNS = SLG_ZNS
        this.SLG_VZD = SLG_VZD
        for (var i = 0; i < arrayKombinacije.length; i++)
        {
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK2 = SLF_FAK2;
            arrayKombinacije[i].SLF_FAK3 = SLF_FAK3;
        }
    }

    function SkrijKontrole(SLG_DAV)
    {
        if (SLG_DAV > 0) {
            GetElement('divListekDavekNaDobitek').style.display = '';
            GetElement('divListekZaIzplacilo').style.display = '';
            GetElement('divListekDavekNaDobitek').className  = 'eventDetails ticketTax';
            GetElement('divListekZaIzplacilo').className  = 'eventDetails ticketPayout';
        }
        else {
            GetElement('divListekDavekNaDobitek').style.display = 'none';
            GetElement('divListekZaIzplacilo').style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
        

    $(document).ready(function () {
        
        PreracunajDobitek(true, true, true);
    });

    
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var gameService = {

                return "5";

                return "5";

        var external = {
            DoCommand: function (command, args) {
                if (command.toString().toLowerCase() == "messagedlg") {
                    iPos = args.indexOf(';');

                    if (iPos == -1)
                        setTimeout(function () { showAlert('Obvestilo', args) }, 0);
                    else
                        setTimeout(function () { showAlert('Obvestilo', args.substring(0, iPos)) }, 0);
                }

                if (command.toString().toLowerCase() == "login") {
                    if (parent.inputPars.Origin() == '5') {
                        var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
                        xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
                            if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
                                var jHTML = eval('(' + xmlhttp.responseText + ')');
                                if (jHTML[0].UserInfo.user.OIRG_VRE) {
                                }
                                else {
                                    showAlert('Napaka', 'Vnesite uporabniško ime in geslo, če še niste registrirani pa izberite "Postani član"!')
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if (xmlhttp) {
                            xmlhttp.open('GET', '/REST.aspx?action=UserInfo&RCE_TIP=22&json=true', true);
                            xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
                            xmlhttp.send();
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        showLogin();
                    }
                }

                if ((command.toString().toLowerCase() == "podatkiir") || (command.toString().toLowerCase() == "balance")) {
                    
                    getUserInfo();

                    if (opener == null)
                        return;

                    if (typeof (opener.StanjeKonta == 'function'))
                        opener.StanjeKonta(args);

                }
                if (command.toString().toLowerCase() == "egameservice")
                    return gameService.Url();
                if (command.toString().toLowerCase() == "odgovornoigranje") {
                    if (typeof miniIgraOdgovornoIgranje == 'function') {
                        miniIgraOdgovornoIgranje();
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        var userAuth = false;

        function AuthCheck() {
            try {
                console.warn("function AuthCheck() is depricated! Use service authentication data instead!");
            }
            catch (e) { }
            if (userAuth)
                return true;
            else
                external.DoCommand('login');

        }
		
        function refreshUser() {
            try {
                console.warn("function refreshUser() is depricated!");
            }
            catch (e) { }
            external.DoCommand('podatkiir');

        }

        function getUserInfo() {
            
            try {
                if (inputPars.Origin() == '5') {
                    parent.Prijava_StanjeKonta();
                    return;
                }
            }
            catch (e) { }
            try {
                if (parent.inputPars.Origin() == '5') {
                    parent.Prijava_StanjeKonta();
                    return;
                }
            }
            catch (e) { }

                var UserData = GetElement('UserData');

                if (UserData) {
                    var xmlhttp = GetXmlHttpObject();
                    xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function () {
                        if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
                            var jHTML = eval('(' + xmlhttp.responseText + ')');
                            if (jHTML[0].UserInfo.user.OIRG_VRE) {
                                UserData.innerHTML = jHTML[0].UserInfo.user.OIRG_NIK;
                                UserData.innerHTML += "<br/>" + jHTML[0].UserInfo.user.OIRG_VRE;
                                userAuth = true;
                                UserData.className = "eGamesKonto";
                            }
                            else {
                                UserData.innerHTML = "Prijava";
                                userAuth = false;
                                UserData.className = "eGamesBtn";
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    if (xmlhttp) {
                        xmlhttp.open('GET', '/REST.aspx?action=UserInfo&RCE_TIP=22&json=true', true);
                        xmlhttp.setRequestHeader('If-Modified-Since', 'Sat, 1 Jan 2000 00:00:00 GMT');
                        xmlhttp.send();
                    }

                }
            
        }
        function resizeIframe() {
            if (inputPars.Origin() == '5') {
                var iframe = document.getElementById('ctl12_Modul5644_frameIgra');
                var header = document.getElementById('eGameHeader');

                var ratio = 1.3;

                var frmDoc = iframe.contentDocument || iframe.contentWindow.document;
                var canvas = frmDoc.getElementsByTagName("canvas");
                if (canvas.length > 0) {
                    ratio = canvas[0].height / canvas[0].width;
                }
                var calcW = $("#ctl12_Modul5644_frameIgra").css('width');
                var calcH = parseInt(calcW) * ratio;

                iframe.style.height = calcH;
                iframe.height = calcH;

            }
            else {
                var iframe = document.getElementById('ctl12_Modul5644_frameIgra');
                var header = document.getElementById('eGameHeader');

                var w = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientWidth, window.innerWidth || 0)
                var h = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0)

                if (h > 0 && header)
                    h = (h - header.offsetHeight);

                if (document.getElementsByTagName("iframe")[0].height != '100%') {

                    w = w - 5;
                    h = h - 5;
                }

                iframe.style.width = w;
                iframe.style.height = h;
                iframe.width = w;
                iframe.height = h;

                try {

                    if (iframe.contentWindow != null) {
                        iframe.contentWindow.width = w;
                        iframe.contentWindow.height = h;

                    }
                }
                catch (e) {
                }
            }

        }

        function goBack() {

                try {
                    window.close();
                    return;
                }
                catch (e) { }

                try {
                    var win = window.open('', '_self', '');
                    win.close();
                    return;
                }
                catch (ex) { }

                window.history.go(-1);

        }

        window.onload = function () {
            
            if (document.getElementsByTagName("iframe")[0].height == '100%') {
                if ('https://igre.e-stave.com/Webgames/Games/Akvarij5/HTML5Game/index.html?dummy=636429666429002344&Game=Akvarij5&Lang=SLO&GameEnv=web' != "")
                    document.getElementsByTagName("iframe")[0].src = 'https://igre.e-stave.com/Webgames/Games/Akvarij5/HTML5Game/index.html?dummy=636429666429002344&Game=Akvarij5&Lang=SLO&GameEnv=web';

            }

            resizeIframe();

            getUserInfo();

        }

       

        function attachEventHandler(element, eventToHandle, eventHandler) {
            if (element.attachEvent) {
                element.attachEvent(eventToHandle, eventHandler);
            } else if (element.addEventListener) {
                element.addEventListener(eventToHandle.replace("on", ""), eventHandler, false);
            } else {
                element[eventToHandle] = eventHandler;
            }
        }

        attachEventHandler(window, "onresize", function () {
            resizeIframe();
        });

    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function rk_bannerUpdateXMLRequest(bannerID, strURL) {
    	console.info(bannerID, strURL);
    	var xmlBannerReq = false;
		var self = null;

		if(document.getElementById(bannerID) != null) {
			self = document.getElementById(bannerID);
			// Mozilla/Safari
			if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
				self.xmlBannerReq = new XMLHttpRequest();
			}
			// IE
			else if (window.ActiveXObject) {
				self.xmlBannerReq = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
			}
			console.info("OK**********************");
			self.xmlBannerReq.open('GET', strURL, true);
			self.xmlBannerReq.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
			self.xmlBannerReq.onreadystatechange = function() {
				if (self.xmlBannerReq.readyState == 4) {
					self.xmlBannerReq.close;

					if (self.xmlBannerReq.status == 200){
						rk_updateActiveBanner(bannerID, self.xmlBannerReq.responseXML);
						console.info("BANNER UPDATED" + self.xmlBannerReq.responseXML);
					}
				}
			}
			self.xmlBannerReq.send(null);
			console.info(self.xmlBannerReq.responseText);
		}
	}

	function rk_updateActiveBanner(bannerID, xmlDoc) {

		var dobitek = 0;

		//if(document.getElementById(bannerID) != null) {
			if(xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("data")[0].getAttribute("dobitek") > 0) {
				//console.info("UPDATING: " + document.getElementById(bannerID+"-txt"));
				//document.getElementById(bannerID).setAttribute("class","MiniAd-display");
				document.getElementById(bannerID).style.display = "block";
				document.getElementById(bannerID).className = "MiniAd-display";
				document.getElementById(bannerID+"-txt").style.display = "block";
				var dobitekStr = xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("data")[0].getAttribute("dobitek");
				var dobitek = parseFloat(dobitekStr.replace(/\./g, ""));
				//var dobitek = parseFloat(dobitekStr.replace(/\s/g, "").replace(",", "."));
				//alert("DOBITEK : " + dobitek);
				document.getElementById(bannerID+"-txt").innerHTML =  "<span id='"+ bannerID+"-num" +"' class='"+ bannerID+"-num" + "'>0</span>"+"<span id='activeAdCurrency' class='activeAdCurrency'>€</span>";
				var dot_separator_number_step = $.animateNumber.numberStepFactories.separator('.');
				$("#"+bannerID+"-num").animateNumber({ number: dobitek, numberStep: dot_separator_number_step });
				document.getElementById(bannerID+"-krog").innerHTML = "Krog: " + xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("data")[0].getAttribute("krog") + "<br>" + xmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("data")[0].getAttribute("datumkroga");
			} else {
				document.getElementById(bannerID).style.display = "none";
			}
		//}
	}

	function toggleVertMenu() {
		if(vertMenuVisible) {
			$('#column01').animate({
				left: '-220px',
			}, 500 );
			vertMenuVisible = false;
		} else {
			$('#column01').animate({
				left: '0px',
			}, 500 );
			vertMenuVisible = true;
		}
	}

<script type='text/javascript'>
(function ($) {
            
            var SHOW_ALLWAYS = true;
            
            function checkScrolling(colID, colWidth)
            {
               
                var distFooter = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).innerHeight() - $('#footer_container').position().top;
                var height = $(window).innerHeight();
               
               if ($('#headerwrapper').css('position') == 'fixed')
               {
                    /** plavajoči header **/ 
                    $(colID + ' .restraint').css('position', 'fixed');
                    $(colID + ' .restraint').css('width', colWidth);
                
                     if (distFooter > 0)
                        height = height - distFooter +  $('#headerwrapper').height();
                
                    /***********************/ 
                }
                else
                {
                    /*** Če je header na vrhu strani ***/
                
                    if ($(this).scrollTop() > $('#headerwrapper').height()) {
                        $(colID + ' .restraint').addClass('scrolling');
                        $(colID + ' .restraint').css('width', colWidth);
                            
                    } else {
                        $(colID + ' .restraint').removeClass('scrolling');
                        height = $(window).innerHeight() - ($('#headerwrapper').height() - $(this).scrollTop()) ;                          
                    }
                
                    /************************/
                }
               
                
                if (distFooter > 0)
                    height = height - distFooter;
                $(colID + ' .restraint .scroller').css('max-height',height );
                $(colID + ' .restraint .scroller').css('height', height);
                $(colID + ' .restraint .scroller .mCSB_inside').css('max-height',height );
                 
            }


            function prepairScrolling(colID)
            {
               
                var distFooter = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).innerHeight() - $('#footer_container').position().top;
                var height = $(window).innerHeight() - $('#headerwrapper').height();
                if (distFooter > 0)
                    height = height - distFooter;
   
                if ($(colID + ' .restraint .scroller').length > 0) //pogoj za scrollanje column1
                {
                    $(colID).css('height', 10);
                    $(colID + ' .restraint').addClass('side_column');
                                        
                    $(colID + ' .restraint .scroller').css('max-height', height);
                    if (colID == "#column03")
                        $('#column03 .restraint .scroller').css('padding-right',13);
                    

                    //$.mCustomScrollbar.defaults.scrollButtons.enable=true;

                    var _theme = 'minimal-dark';
                    if (SHOW_ALLWAYS)
                        _theme = 'dark-thin';
                        

                    $(colID + ' .restraint .scroller').mCustomScrollbar({
                        theme: _theme,
                        scrollInertia: 500,
                        
                    });

                    //če kažemo fixne drsnike(se ne skrivajo) -theme dark
                    if (SHOW_ALLWAYS)
                    {
                        $('.scroller .padding').css('padding-right',0);
                        $('.mCSB_inside > .mCSB_container').css('margin-right',15);
                    }
                    
                    return true;
                }

                return false;
            }

            $(window).load(function () {
				var col1W = $('#column01 .restraint').width();
                var col1H = $('#column01 .restraint').height();
                var col2H = $('#column02 .restraint').height();
                var col3W = $('#column03 .restraint').width();
                var col3H = $('#column03 .restraint').height();

                if (prepairScrolling('#column01'))
                {
                    checkScrolling('#column01', col1W)
                    $(window).scroll(function () {
                    
                        checkScrolling('#column01', col1W)
                        
                    });
                }

                if (prepairScrolling('#column03'))                   
                {
                    checkScrolling('#column03', col3W)
                    $(window).scroll(function () {
                    
                        checkScrolling('#column03', col3W)
                        
                    });
                }
                

            });
        })(jQuery);</script>

<script language='javascript'>
    // Start trapping mouse

    //if (document.layers) document.captureEvents(Event.MOUSEMOVE);
    //document.onmousemove=mtrack;
    
    var okvir; //floating div
    var ttop; 
    var tmiddle; 
    var ent; 
    var tbottom; 
    var posx=0; // mouseX
    var posy=0; // mouseY
    var offsetX=0; // Offset X away from mouse
    var offsetY=-5; // Offset Y
    var popUp = false; // Is it showing right now??!
	  var lastLeft = "-500px"; //zadnja pozicija balona
	  var lastTop = "-500px"; //zadnja pozicija balona
	  var lastText = ""; //zadnji text
    var oblacekElem = null;

    // Run upon load
    function init() {
    // Set up div we will use to hover our text
    okvir = document.createElement("div");
    okvir.id = "tooltip";

    ttop.className = "ttop";

        GetElement("FormPortal").appendChild(okvir);
