<script language='javascript'>
function getScrollXY() {

      var scrOfX = 0, scrOfY = 0;
      if( typeof( window.pageYOffset ) == 'number' ) {
        //Netscape compliant
        scrOfY = window.pageYOffset;
        scrOfX = window.pageXOffset;
      } else if( document.body && ( document.body.scrollLeft || document.body.scrollTop ) ) {
        //DOM compliant
        scrOfY = document.body.scrollTop;
        scrOfX = document.body.scrollLeft;
      } else if( document.documentElement && ( document.documentElement.scrollLeft || document.documentElement.scrollTop ) ) {
        //IE6 standards compliant mode
        scrOfY = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        scrOfX = document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
      }
      return [ scrOfX, scrOfY ];
    }

    // Keeps mouse x and y in posx and posy

    function mtrack(e) 
    {
        if (popUp) 
        {
            if (!e)
                 e = window.event;
            if (e.pageX || e.pageY) 
            {
                posx = e.pageX;
                posy = e.pageY;
            }
            else if (e.clientX || e.clientY) 
            {
                posx = e.clientX;
                posy = e.clientY;
            }
            //posx = getScrollXY()[0] + posx;
            //posy = getScrollXY()[1] + posy;
            if (isIE())
            {
                posleft = posx + offsetX + getScrollXY()[0];
                postop = posy + offsetY + getScrollXY()[1];
             }
             else
             {
                posleft = posx + offsetX; 
                postop = posy + offsetY; 
             }
             
            if(okvir != null)
            {
                // širina okna z vsebino je 980
                //if ((posleft + ent.offsetWidth) > 980)
                  //  posleft = 980 - ent.offsetWidth;
                okvir.style.left = (posleft).toString()+"px";
                okvir.style.top = postop.toString()+"px";
                
            }
        }
    }
    // Change floating div to correct text on mouseover

    function doOblacekText(t, e, is_okvir)
    {
      oblacekElem = e;
      if(okvir != null && (!is_okvir || !popUp))
      {
          if (!is_okvir)
		    { 
			    ent.innerHTML = t;
			    okvir.style.left = (getLeft(e) + e.clientWidth + offsetX + 5) + "px";
			    okvir.style.top = (getTop(e) + offsetY )+"px";
			    lastLeft = okvir.style.left;
			    lastTop = okvir.style.top;
			    lastText = ent.innerHTML;
		    }
		    else
		    {
			    ent.innerHTML = lastText;
			    okvir.style.left = lastLeft;
			    okvir.style.top = lastTop;
		    }
          //ent.style.visibility = 'visible';
          okvir.style.display = 'block';
          ent.style.display = 'block';
          ttop.style.display = 'block';
          tbottom.style.display = 'block';
          tmiddle.style.display = 'block';
		    //alert(getLeft(e) + " " + getWidth(e));
		    
          //ttop.style.visibility = 'visible';
          //tmiddle.style.visibility = 'visible';
          //tbottom.style.visibility = 'visible';
          popUp = true;
      }
      itimer = setInterval(function () {doOblacekClear()}, 10000);
  }
    // Change back to nothing

    function doOblacekClear() {
    popUp = false;
    oblacekElem = null;
    if(ent != null)
    {
        okvir.style.left = -500;
        okvir.style.top = -500;
        //okvir.style.visibility = 'hidden';
        okvir.style.display = 'none';
        ent.style.display = 'none';
        ttop.style.display = 'none';
        tbottom.style.display = 'none';
        tmiddle.style.display = 'none';
        ent.innerHTML = "";
    }
     clearInterval(itimer)
    }
    function isIE()
    {
      return /msie/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/opera/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
    }
    function switchToolTip(t, e)
    {
      if (popUp)
          doOblacekClear();
      else
          doOblacekText(t, e, false);
    }
</script>
